< review>
This review is coming in a little late as life got in the way. However, what I can say is I've been driving in my car that I Kim's Auto Body repaired and I've had no issues after 1.5 months.

My Mazda 6 was involved in an accident where my front bumper was crushed in towards the engine, the radiator supports were bent, the sensors behind the bumper were affected amongst other things. Initially, my insurance strongly advised me to work with their recommended body shops. I did my research and chose Kim's Auto Body. I don't know much about cars and I found James to be honest, thorough in his explanation and patient. He walked me through the whole process, explained what parts would be best to go with, whether to take the insurance downgrades, etc.

In the end, I received my car with it looking and driving like it was never involved in an accident. I even got to test the front safety sensors when a car in front of me stopped short and I had to brake suddenly. I'm grateful all the safety features work as expected.

I would absolutely recommend Kim's Auto Body for their professional service and quality of work.< /review>

< Review>
I was in the bay area on business and had a few too many at a business lunch in chinatown, stumbled out into the bright daylight and dialed up an uber on my phone. It arrived and I fell asleep in the back. I guess I put in the wrong address because we ended up here, where I woke up to the driver yelling at me to get out. I obliged him and before i got my bearings he had driven away. The pumpkin patch was closed, but I was intrigued and stumbled in. As I wandered amongst the pumpkins and gourds, I just couldn't comprehend such a thing in alameda. My head started to hurt so I laid down on some straw bales and took a little rest while I waited for my lyft driver to arrive, which he shortly did - clearly amused and curious how I found myself there. He was discrete however and didn't inquire, so we rode in silence.

I had actually forgotten about this until google suggested I review the place and it all came flooding back.

Three stars only due to it not being open and the sense of existential dread and confusion the experience caused. Good for kids.</Review>

Firstly, I found the staff friendly and helpful and therefore this review is not directed at any individual at the facility but to the corporation of Public Storage.
I rented the space 13 months ago for $257 per month and moved in my belongings. At that time, I was disturbed to see a group of people nearby wearing masks as they moved out contents from another unit. I was curious and asked the lady what was so hazardous that they were wearing masks. She explained that the unit was rat infested and a lot of damage was sustained to their belongings as a result. I was disturbed by this news but tried to reassure myself that there were no holes in my unit where rats could enter. Later I realized I was mistaken!
The reason I finally left the unit was due to 2 rent increases within a year. The first after 4 months from $257 to $317. The second came 8 months later taking the rent from $317 to $416. overall that is a 62% increase within a year. I was a good tenant and the rent was paid by direct debit.
I decided quickly and moved my stuff out: It was then that I found that my unit was also rat infested and swarming ants too.  Rat droppings and urine stains everywhere. Most of my belongings were safely boxed however; but mattresses and bedding were not and suffered. I estimated the damage at $700.

I believe that there is a breach of contract in Public Storage's failure to exercise duty of care towards their tenants' health and property. I would advise others, who may need temporary storage of their belongings, to think twice before using this facility.
They are not even worthy of one star in this review.<//text>
